Holding\n  risks the full −1.5% loss; exiting now saves ~₹5.30/share.\n\n  [ ✓ Approve ]  [ ✗ Reject ]\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThree consent modes — \u003cstrong\u003ein-chat\u003c/strong\u003e (you're present), \u003cstrong\u003easync\u003c/strong\u003e (agent queues while you're away), \u003cstrong\u003eautonomous\u003c/strong\u003e (within guardrails you define upfront in the Playbook).\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003chr\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"markdown-heading\" dir=\"auto\"\u003e\u003ch2 tabindex=\"-1\" class=\"heading-element\" dir=\"auto\"\u003eEvery decision on record. - Strategy is now a pure document (no state/status fields)
- Portfolio drops benchmark/strategyIds; PortfolioStore drops addStrategy/removeStrategy
- StrategyStore: list() returns all, delete() replaces setStatus/setState
- ApprovalStore: list() with no filter returns all approvals (newest first)

- Order sync runs on every tick (not just post-reasoning)
- TradeArgs gains product_type (CNC/INTRADAY); hard orders default to DELIVERY
- runner: add get_portfolio_holdings tool for long-term equity holdings

- create_strategy: drop state/status params
- list_strategies: return all (no active filter)
- register_trigger: expiresAt past-date validation; intentId param; product_type in tradeArgs

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Vibe Trade</h1><a id="user-content-vibe-trade" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Vibe Trade" href="#vibe-trade"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Your portfolio. Your strategy. Running itself.</strong></p>
<p dir="auto">Vibe Trade is a local AI trading agent powered by Claude. Describe your strategy in plain English — the agent writes the Playbook, builds the automation stack, monitors the market around the clock, and comes to you with a reasoned case before touching your account.</p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="/vibetrade-ai/vibe-trade/blob/main/LICENSE"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/68951403553b4bae256e8b7cf81c8875f43d6050853ccf51d0d025dc3eadf008/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f6c6963656e73652d4d49542d3444464634443f6c6162656c436f6c6f723d313131" alt="License: MIT" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/license-MIT-4DFF4D?labelColor=111" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Talk to your portfolio — with live data</h2><a id="user-content-talk-to-your-portfolio--with-live-data" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Talk to your portfolio — with live data" href="#talk-to-your-portfolio--with-live-data"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Ask the agent anything. It has 20 built-in tools and a live broker connection. It fetches real prices, reads your open positions, pulls candles and indicators, and scans the news — then answers like a portfolio manager who's been watching all morning.</p>

<p dir="auto">No stale training data. No hallucinated prices. Every answer grounded in what's actually happening right now.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Write a strategy once. Run it forever.</h2><a id="user-content-write-a-strategy-once-run-it-forever" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Write a strategy once. Run it forever." href="#write-a-strategy-once-run-it-forever"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Describe your thesis in plain English. The agent shapes it into a <strong>Playbook</strong> — entry rules, exit criteria, capital allocation, guardrails — and from that point, every decision it makes is anchored to that document.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto"><pre class="notranslate"><code>you:   Intraday momentum strategy, long and short. Three concurrent

<p dir="auto">Same rules. Every session. No drift, no forgotten instructions, consistent P&amp;L tracking against the thesis.</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">The agent builds its own automation stack</h2><a id="user-content-the-agent-builds-its-own-automation-stack" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: The agent builds its own automation stack" href="#the-agent-builds-its-own-automation-stack"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">When a position opens, the agent immediately registers the full set of triggers to manage it — stop-losses, targets, trailing stops, monitors, re-entry scanners. You describe the risk model once in the Playbook. The agent wires it up.</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Always watching. Only thinking when it matters.</h2><a id="user-content-always-watching-only-thinking-when-it-matters" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Always watching. Only thinking when it matters." href="#always-watching-only-thinking-when-it-matters"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Heartbeat</strong> monitors your positions and triggers every 30 seconds — without running the LLM. Price conditions are evaluated in pure JavaScript. Cron handles time-based triggers. The expensive model only wakes up when something actually fires.</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Nothing happens without your say-so</h2><a id="user-content-nothing-happens-without-your-say-so" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Nothing happens without your say-so" href="#nothing-happens-without-your-say-so"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Before any order is placed, the agent submits a structured approval card — not a chat message. The exact trade, and every signal that led to the recommendation. You approve or reject. The gate is code-level; there is no way around it.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto"><pre class="notranslate"><code>  APPROVAL REQUEST · Aggressive Alpha — Position Monitor

<p dir="auto">Three consent modes — <strong>in-chat</strong> (you're present), <strong>async</strong> (agent queues while you're away), <strong>autonomous</strong> (within guardrails you define upfront in the Playbook).</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Every decision on record. Permanently.</h2><a id="user-content-every-decision-on-record-permanently" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Every decision on record. Permanently." href="#every-decision-on-record-permanently"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Every trade is written to an immutable journal with the agent's reasoning at the moment of decision — not a post-hoc summary. Every trigger run is logged, including runs where no trade was placed. Ask the agent to explain any past decision and it has the full context.</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">How it works</h2><a id="user-content-how-it-works" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: How it works" href="#how-it-works"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Vibe Trade is built on six primitives. Each one solves a problem an LLM can't solve on its own.</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto"><pre class="notranslate"><code>Heartbeat → snapshot → Trigger fires → Playbook loaded
  → LLM reasons → Permissions gate → Trade placed → Learnings logs
</code></pre><div class="zeroclipboard-container">
    <clipboard-copy aria-label="Copy code to clipboard" class="ClipboardButton btn btn-invisible js-clipboard-copy m-2 p-0 d-flex flex-justify-center flex-items-center" data-copy-feedback="Copied!" data-tooltip-direction="w" value="Heartbeat → snapshot → Trigger fires → Playbook loaded
  → LLM reasons → Permissions gate → Trade placed → Learnings logs" tabindex="0" role="button">
      <svg aria-hidden="true" data-component="Octicon" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-copy js-clipboard-copy-icon">
    <path d="M0 6.75C0 5.784.784 5 1.75 5h1.5a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.5h-1.5a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25v7.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h7.5a.25.25 0 0 0 .25-.25v-1.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0v1.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 9.25 16h-7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 0 14.25Z"></path><path d="M5 1.75C5 .784 5.784 0 6.75 0h7.5C15.216 0 16 .784 16 1.75v7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.25 11h-7.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 5 9.25Zm1.75-.25a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25v7.5c0 .138.112.25.25.25h7.5a.25.25 0 0 0 .25-.25v-7.5a.25.25 0 0 0-.25-.25Z"></path>
</svg>
      <svg aria-hidden="true" data-component="Octicon" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-check js-clipboard-check-icon color-fg-success d-none">
    <path d="M13.78 4.22a.75.75 0 0 1 0 1.06l-7.25 7.25a.75.75 0 0 1-1.06 0L2.22 9.28a.751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018L6 10.94l6.72-6.72a.75.75 0 0 1 1.06 0Z"></path>
</svg>
    </clipboard-copy>
  </div></div>
<markdown-accessiblity-table data-catalyst=""><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>#</th>
<th>Primitive</th>
<th>What it gives the agent</th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>01</td>
<td><strong>Market Tooling</strong></td>
<td>20 tools — live quotes, candles, indicators, fundamentals, news, order book, broker execution</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>02</td>
<td><strong>Heartbeat</strong></td>
<td>30s monitoring loop — evaluates all trigger conditions without running the LLM</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>03</td>
<td><strong>Triggers</strong></td>
<td>Condition + action. Modes: <code>code</code> <code>event</code> <code>time</code> <code>llm</code>. Types: <code>hard_order</code> <code>reasoning_job</code></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>04</td>
<td><strong>Permissions</strong></td>
<td>Code-level approval gate — three consent modes, full audit trail</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>05</td>
<td><strong>Playbooks</strong></td>
<td>Persistent strategy document — consistent identity, isolated P&amp;L, capital bounds</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>06</td>
<td><strong>Learnings</strong></td>
<td>Immutable trade journal — reasoning captured at decision time, not reconstructed after</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>07</td>
<td><strong>Skills</strong></td>
<td>Reusable instruction modules per Playbook <em>(coming soon)</em></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<p dir="auto">→ <a href="https://vibetrade-ai.github.io/docs" rel="nofollow">Full documentation</a></p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Quickstart</h2><a id="user-content-quickstart" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Quickstart" href="#quickstart"><svg data-component="Octicon" class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Requirements</strong></p>
<markdown-accessiblity-table data-catalyst=""><table>
<thead>
<tr>
<th>Dependency</th>
<th></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Node.js ≥ 20</td>
<td>Runtime</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Anthropic API key</td>
<td>Claude Sonnet for reasoning jobs, Haiku for condition evaluation</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Dhan account</td>
<td>Broker — credentials added at <code>/settings</code></td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table></markdown-accessiblity-table>
<p dir="auto">Vibe Trade is designed to support multiple brokers. We're starting with <strong>Dhan</strong> — more brokers are on the roadmap.</p>
<p dir="auto">Add your Anthropic API key and Dhan credentials at <code>http://localhost:3001/settings</code> once the server is running.</p>
<p dir="auto">Everything runs on your machine. Your API key, credentials, trade history, and Playbooks never leave your local environment — stored in <code>~/.vibetrade/</code>.</p>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Start with chat before automation.</strong> Ask the agent to look at your positions, fetch a quote, explain a stock's technicals. Once you're comfortable with how it reasons and what tools it has, give it a Playbook and let it run.</p>
</blockquote>
<hr>
